Murder Case of Gao Qiao Cracked

Adulterous Woman and Murderer Both Detained

Last summer, a case occurred where Zhang Jinmao, a native of Gao Qiao Town in Pudong and a foreman at the Texaco Oil Company, was murdered and his body dumped in the river. The Third District Fourth Precinct, considering it a murder case with the perpetrator at large, reported it to their superiors and issued a strict order for apprehension. Now, almost a year has passed, and the murderer had not been caught, leading many to believe the injustice would remain buried forever. However, recently, Captain Lu of the Shanghai Public Security Bureau's Detective Squad received a confidential report from Detective Zhang Quanzhou, stating that the suspect, named Fu Peisheng, was currently hiding with his mistress, Zhang Gao (also known as Mao Lang), at No. 12 Hui Ning Road in the South City. Captain Lu, upon receiving the report, first summoned the deceased's father, Zhang Shaoyun, to the station for detailed questioning. According to Zhang Shaoyun, his son Jinmao had been living with his mistress Gao (also known as Mao Lang) in Gao Qiao Town. He worked as a foreman at Texaco, leaving early and returning late, which was his usual routine. A man named Fu Peisheng, whom he had known, was imprisoned in the 16th year due to a case. After his release, having no home to return to, Jinmao invited him to live in his house. Unexpectedly, Gao was of a romantic nature and, taking advantage of Jinmao's absence during the day, gradually began an affair with Fu Peisheng. Furthermore, Jinmao was always enthusiastic about public affairs in Gao Qiao, especially regarding theft cases, where he would do his best to assist the authorities in solving them. Therefore, he was deeply resented by bandits. Two days before his death, while he was drinking tea in the Qujiaqiao teahouse, Fu Peisheng suddenly said, "Although your son Jinmao is currently catching robbers with the Gaoqiao police, there are many robbers, and he will be beaten to death by them in the future." Unexpectedly, on the night of the eleventh, Jinmao was murdered. The next day, he went to Gao's residence to inquire, but she had already fled, and Fu Peisheng was also nowhere to be found. Following these clues, Fu Peisheng was deemed to be highly suspicious. Detective Hu Kui-sheng, Cui You-kuan, Gu You-san, Han Feng-ying, and Xia Xiu-ying were dispatched, along with police officers from the Second District, to arrest Fu Peisheng and Zhang Gao and bring them back to the station for separate interrogations. Fu confessed that during the fourth month of the previous lunar year, he had an affair with Zhang Gao. He initially knew nothing about Zhang Jinmao's murder. The next day, Mao Lang came to Shanghai and found him at his sister's place, where he learned about it. Later, due to rumors that anyone acquainted with Zhang Jinmao would be arrested, he fled with Mao Lang, first to Hankou, then back to Nanjing, and then from Nanjing back to Shanghai, eventually fleeing to Jiaxing. Only at the end of November did they return to Shanghai. When questioned, Zhang Gao confessed that on the night of the incident, she and Jinmao had already gone to sleep when two men came upstairs and asked Jinmao to come outside to talk. At that time, Jinmao instructed her to follow him downstairs. However, after walking a few steps out the door, she saw that there was another man and woman waiting there. She then saw Jinmao walking ahead with the two men who had come upstairs, while she followed behind with the other man and woman. Unexpectedly, as she passed Qujiaqiao, she suddenly heard a sound like a small cannon, and immediately the woman told her, "Zhang Jinmao has been killed by them." She screamed for help but they stuffed her mouth, etc. After hearing the confessions, Captain Lu believed that although Fu Peisheng and the others did not confess to the murder, their act of fleeing with Zhang Gao from Hankou to Nanjing to Shanghai to Zhejiang clearly indicated guilt and evasion. At the same time, it was also discovered that the suspect was also significantly involved in the case of Yuan Erlang and other robbers that the Third District Fourth Precinct had submitted last autumn. He was also wanted by the Songhu Garrison Headquarters. Therefore, the suspect was not only suspected of murder but was also a fugitive robber. Therefore, he prepared a document and sent them to the Public Security Bureau for interrogation.

Boy Crushed to Death by Car

Xu Dongtai, the son of a Xu family residing at No. 3 Rong Qing Li, Maite He Si Tu Road, Public Concession, was only ten years old. Yesterday afternoon at 4:30, he was wandering alone on the road in front of his house when he was suddenly hit by a car with license plate number 13796, causing a head injury and rendering him unconscious. He was seen by a constable from the Gordon Road Police Station, who immediately arrested the driver, Liu Haicuo, and detained him at the police station. He will be handed over to the court tomorrow morning for punishment. The injured child was carried by the police to Bao Long Hospital for treatment, but to no avail. He died at 8:30 in the evening.

Foreigner's Car Crashes Violently into Rickshaw

Passenger Barely Breathing

Rickshaw Puller Unconscious

Yesterday evening around 10:45, near the eastern end of the Xiafei Road Songshan Road Police Station, a rickshaw carrying a pedestrian in his twenties was traveling west to east. A foreigner, accompanied by a foreign woman, was driving their private car, license number 7511 (registered in the Concession), at high speed. When they reached the location, they violently crashed into the back of the rickshaw. The rickshaw was severely damaged, and the rickshaw puller was thrown over ten feet, falling to the ground unconscious. The passenger's abdomen was run over by the car's wheels, and he was barely breathing. A constable at the police station entrance witnessed the accident, recorded the car's license plate number, and rushed the injured to Renji Hospital for treatment. It is said that the injuries of both were so severe that their lives were in danger.

Woman Falls into River and Drowns Due to Loss of Footing

Yao Maomao, a boat dweller at the pier, usually docks his boat near the Xin Lajiqiao embankment. On the 4th of this month, his wife Yao Zhou (age 40) was washing rice for cooking, and stepped on the edge of the boat. Unexpectedly, she became dizzy, lost her footing, and fell into the river. The water patrol immediately attempted a rescue, but without success. Only yesterday was her body recovered at the same location, having not drifted away. The water patrol ordered that the local court be notified for an inquest.

Gradual Improvement Expected in Yarn and Cotton Market

The Flower Yarn Market Suspended for One Day on the 5th

Signs of improvement are gradually emerging in the yarn market, requiring even more activity. There is hope for a turnaround in the situation. The Jiangxi merchants, who have been inactive for a long time, have begun purchasing. Therefore, the current yarn market situation is firmer than yesterday. However, demand from other merchant groups remains sluggish. Japanese yarn floods North China, leaving no room for domestic yarn. As for the Japanese-owned yarn factories in this city, their operations are gradually returning to normal, with vigorous activity in the background. This has dealt a significant blow to domestic yarn. Some manufacturers are losing confidence and have no intention of holding firm on current yarn prices, choosing to follow the trend. This may lead to a slight reduction in inventory. However, given the recent sharp decline in prices, a temporary rebound is likely. However, the unstable political situation and stagnant financial conditions are closely related to the yarn market.

Spot Standard Up Five to Six Cents. The spot standard market opened with a tight situation due to the rising prices. In addition, external prices also increased. There was a shortage of sellers in the market, but transactions remained low. Prices for all months rose by five to six cents. The afternoon market was flat, with this month's price rising by one cent, and far-month prices were flat. The total transaction volume for the day was 4,950 bales. Changfeng sold 400 bales, Xiesheng 200 bales, Yiyu 350 bales, Ruidar 700 bales, Yuandar 150 bales, Gengfeng 100 bales, and Zhenda 100 bales. Prices rose by 2.5 to 5 cents, but thread prices remained unchanged. Ningbo merchants purchased 20 bales, Jiangxi merchants 720 bales, inland merchants 90 bales, Guangdong merchants 105 bales, Northern merchants 50 bales, Wuhu merchants 15 bales, Shantou merchants 55 bales, and Fujian merchants 55 bales. Shenxin Factory offered 1200 bales, it is said.

Cotton Market Even More Bullish

The cotton market situation is particularly tight. The continued rise in American cotton prices for several days has improved the yarn market, leading to a stronger cotton market. Due to the low inventory of domestic cotton, there is a shortage of new sellers in the market, pushing prices higher. However, actual demand remains sluggish, and factories are extremely hesitant. Although the price of foreign cotton futures has risen, the weakening exchange rate makes calculations based on silver prices still cheaper than domestic cotton. Therefore, there is no indication of a significant price increase in the market.

Zheng Standard Up Three to Four Cents. The Zheng Standard market opened with rising prices due to increases in both American and Indian cotton. Market sentiment was tight, and there was a shortage of sellers. Prices for all months rose by 2.3 cents. The afternoon situation remained firm, with prices for all months rising by 5 cents. New Green Tea Opens in the Silk, Tea, and Local Produce Market

Local tea factories in this city have been transporting new raw tea from Zhuji, Si'an, Huzhou, and Suian for days, numbering no less than 200 packages. Tea factories such as Tiancheng, Yitongxing, Wanchengxiang, and Wusenji have all started working overtime to produce the first batch of Zhenmei tea from Shaoxing. The new prices were offered by Jardine Matheson and Xiehe companies in the past two days, ranging from 120 to 125 taels. It is reported that large quantities of leaves from Suian and Huzhou, which are of better quality, will be listed on the market one after another next Monday.

New Samples of Qimen Black Tea Arrive in Shanghai

Qimen black tea, yesterday, two new samples were sent from Jiujiang. After the assessment by Jardine Matheson tea experts, it was recognized that the aroma, taste, and strands were even better than last year. However, due to excessive frost last winter, the harvests in all regions were reported to be poor. According to a general survey and estimate by tea merchants, the total output of Qimen, Fuliang, and Jiande this year will be no more than 48,000 boxes, a decrease of about 20% compared to previous years.

Suian Raw Tea Prices Fall

Since the opening of the Suian green tea market on the 27th of last month, the asking price rose to 94 yuan per dan due to strong interest from buyers. Subsequently, due to the vigorous output from various mountain areas, tea merchants also recognized that the tea price was too high and felt it was dangerous. They have gathered to discuss and unanimously suspended the market. As a result, market prices plummeted by 15 to 16 yuan. It is now reported that the local tea merchants and Shanghai merchants have resumed operations, but it has been agreed that tea prices will not be allowed to continue to rise.

Rice Market in Hexia Rises

South Shanghai: Yesterday, there were not many sources from various merchants. Due to weather conditions, people's sentiment was upward. Shops on both sides discussed inventory. The Start of Summer has passed, and rice prices are bound to be firm. Changshu and northern Japonica rice were slightly responsive. The opening price of Bo Dao Pu rice slightly decreased, but inventory was also low. Early rice and foreign Du Jiao were very popular. The situation stabilized. Tong Bian Yin Er Yuan arrived in four packages yesterday and were all sold on the same day. Prices jumped by about 23 cents.

North Shanghai: Yesterday, there were more than ten sources from the interior. The demand in urban and rural stores was not very active. Changshu and northern Japonica rice and Kunshan rice each rose by 10 cents. The demand for Bo Dao Ning rice turned weaker. The local street moved slightly, and prices also increased by 5 cents. There were very few foreign Lu Jiao goods, and the situation was stable. The demand for Tong Bian Yin Hua wine was still good. The opening price rose sharply by nearly 10 cents.

Large Amount of Foreign Rice for Military Needs

The Yangtze River Hinterland Market is also Smooth

Yesterday, the foreign rice market was extremely active. Hankou, Jiangbei, Chongming, Wuxi, Nanjing, and local retailers all made inquiries. The market situation greatly improved. Due to the need to increase shipping costs next week, the Hankou merchants were loading a lot of goods daily. Yesterday, there was even a demand for military rice, further improving the market outlook. The total market opening volume was over 15,000. However, there have been successive arrivals of goods recently. Within the next ten days, 150,000 bags of various types of rice are expected to arrive. Therefore, although sales are active, prices have not been able to rise. Yesterday's opening price for small bags was 10.03 to 10.005 yuan. The market price for special grade small bags was once as high as 10.04 yuan and 10.038 yuan, but there were no transactions. 1,000 bags of Saigon No. 1 rice were priced at 11.5 yuan, and 500 bags of small bag brown rice were priced at 9.4 yuan. Also, 410 bags of Jiangxi Chen Yuan rice were priced at 13.48 yuan and 11.79 yuan.

Flour Market Boosted by Foreign Wheat

Yesterday's foreign wheat telegrams reported uniform increases in both Zhili and Henan, rising by 50 cents and 30 cents respectively. The flour market situation improved slightly, and the north experienced some demand. After the sharp price drop the day before, this aroused interest between local merchants and customers. Lower-grade flours were also sold. The opening price for May Standard Flour was as high as 2.02 yuan, then 2.03 yuan at closing, significantly higher than the previous market. The old Chepai brand opened at 2.0275 yuan. The situation seems likely to stabilize temporarily.

Sugar Market: Coarse Sand and White Sugar Suddenly Rise to Thirteen Taels

Bargain Trading Quite Smooth

The sugar market in the sugar merchants' association was quite active, and the trend was very firm. The price of Dutch Sugar No. 24 coarse sand and white sugar rose to 13 taels. Hong Kong goods were 12 taels and 8.5 qian, later rising to 12 taels and 9 qian. There was a shortage of sellers, and the market atmosphere was quite strong, showing signs of a continued rise. Taikoo sugar was 16 taels and 3.5 qian, DY mark was 15 taels and 3 qian, and HM mark was 13 taels and 7.5 qian, all slightly higher than before, and the market trend was very promising.

The Piece Goods and Cotton Cloth Market is in a State of Peace

The trend of cotton cloth in this factory has stabilized recently. The sales to merchant groups are better in the north. Therefore, heavyweight coarse cloth is quite active. Yesterday, 13-pound Caishen was sold for 6 taels and 2.5 qian, 15-pound Caishen for 7 taels and 3 qian, and 16-pound Shuangyu Jiqing, etc., for more than 200 pieces. The Shantou and Xiamen merchants have purchased very little since the communal strife. Ningbo and Taizhou are also quieter than before. The sales in local stores have improved, so Jin Santa bleached cloth has risen by 5 cents to 8 taels and 5 qian. Local merchants have purchased quite a bit. The trend of fine cloth dyeing factories is wait-and-see, with only sporadic sales in local stores. Blue God, English Blue Chicken, and Balloon are selling better, while fine twill is quite sluggish. Changzhou goods are even quieter, so most are sold for 6 taels and 56 qian. Coarse twill has been quiet again recently, and prices have not changed much. Western piece goods are still sluggish. However, local interest in Elementary Fine Silk is slightly stronger. Yesterday, most of the single-strand and single-yarn products were sold for about 5 qian. Striped patterns are still stagnant.

Progress in the Woolen Fabric Market

Yesterday, the woolen fabric market gradually turned around. Transactions with local merchant groups were more frequent than last week. The political situation has now returned to normal, and credit is gradually easing. Business is developing accordingly. Ordering companies are willing to stamp and release accounts, and they are also very accommodating to small orders, unlike last month when they were unwilling to extend credit. Raincoat cloth, serge, fancy suiting, Zhigong Huate flannel, summer white goods, and French flannel have all been offered by the guild. Unfortunately, the selling prices in the market have not risen. This is due to the relationship between the political situation and the weather.

Hardware Chess Copper Drops Five Qian

Chess copper is a frequently sold item for military factories and Sichuan merchants. The annual sales volume is quite large. However, in recent years, due to the scarcity of goods in the market, prices have risen significantly, currently selling for 185 taels. However, since the price increase, the base price has been too high, causing potential buyers to hesitate, which has greatly impacted transactions. The standard has invisibly dropped by 5 qian, selling for 180 taels. However, there are still few buyers. It is expected that the price may decline further in the future.

New Iron Wire Had Some Movement Yesterday

New iron wire, which has been sluggish for a long time, was more lively yesterday because merchants from Sichuan and Hankou made inquiries. Although the market price has not increased temporarily, market sentiment is good, so there is no tendency to weaken. The current market price for 16 to 20 gauge is 13 taels and 2.5 qian per dan, and 21 to 25 gauge is 14 taels. Investigations have shown that market inventory is extremely low. If business picks up tomorrow, there is a risk of inventory shortages in the future.

Ministry of Education to Hold National Education Administration Conference in the Autumn of This Year

In order to rectify national education administration and improve administrative efficiency, the Ministry of Education plans to convene a National Education Administration Conference this autumn (approximately in September), bringing together the heads of education departments and bureaus from various provinces and cities, as well as administrative district and special district education administrators. It is reported that the regulations are currently being drafted, and preparations will begin after they are approved by the Ministry Affairs Meeting and submitted to the Executive Yuan for approval.

Ministry of Education Commends Individuals Who Donate Funds for Education

The Ministry of Education has issued certificates of commendation to individuals who donated funds for education in various provinces and cities in recent months (from January to the end of April). Excerpts are listed below:

(1) Four individuals were awarded first-class certificates: Hua Yizhi of Wuxi, who donated a total of more than 37,000 yuan to the privately-owned Huaifen Girls' School and the county-run Dangkou Elementary School from August 1926 to July 1931; Li Dengyun of Linyi, Shandong, who founded the privately-owned Xinmin Elementary School in 1929 and donated 150.05 mu of male property to be used as the school's foundation, valued at more than 11,000 yuan; Song Yinghui Hall of Xincai, Henan, who donated 1,515 mu of farmland and 58 houses to the county-run Danwen Elementary School in 1929, worth a total of 100,900 yuan (and a special case was submitted to the National Government for commendation); Chen Lian of Wuxi, who donated a total of 13,000 yuan to the privately-owned Zhihai Elementary School for construction and operating expenses from 1928 to 1931. (2) Three individuals were awarded second-class certificates: Li Clan Hall of Huaining, Anhui, who donated more than 5,000 yuan for the construction of the fifth elementary school in the third school district of the county; Li Shu of Wugang, Hunan, who donated paddy fields valued at 5,000 yuan to the county education bureau; Yang Yizhai of Binchuan, Yunnan, who donated 5,000 yuan for the construction of the provincial middle school library. (3) Six individuals were awarded third-class certificates: Zhang Zizhan of Wuxi, who donated more than 3,000 yuan to the privately-owned Yongbin Elementary School and the county-run Ganlu Elementary School from 1925 to 1931; Liu Yuxiang of Pingdu, Shandong, who donated his privately-owned real estate to the county education bureau for the purpose of running elementary schools in 1931, valued at more than 3,000 yuan; Feng Houcheng Hall of Xixi, Anhui, who donated 3,000 yuan to the privately-owned Yunzhuang Elementary School Foundation; Huang Cuiyue of Meixian, Guangdong, who donated 3,000 yuan for the construction of the fifth provincial middle school; Ying Shushu Academy of Wuxi, who donated a total of more than 4,000 yuan to the county-run Chang'an Bridge Elementary School from 1915 to 1931; You Geshi, who donated 3,000 yuan for the construction of the county-run Dongting Elementary School in 1929.

Xuzhou Middle School Students Disobey Provincial Order to Disband

Dispatched Supervisor Beat, Five Students Sent to County Government for Custody

The situation of the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education temporarily disbanding the senior high school of the Provincial Xuzhou Middle School was reported in yesterday's newspaper. The details are listed below: After the student unrest at Xuzhou Middle School, Supervisor Yi Zuolin, dispatched by the Department of Education, arrived in Xuzhou from Zhenjiang on the evening of the 2nd with Principal Xue Zhongtai. Yi carried a Department order stipulating measures to place five students, Li Gaosong, Li Ruizhu, Ma Guangjun, Yao Hezhang, and Liu Haixi, who were the leaders of the senior high school, under custody pending investigation. Three senior normal school students were expelled, their deposits were confiscated, and tuition and board fees were recovered. All senior high school students were temporarily disbanded and will be reconvened later. Junior high school classes resumed immediately. After arriving in Xuzhou, Yi stayed at the county government and borrowed a company of soldiers from the 7th Division from the military police inspectorate, and mobilized 40 police officers and public security officers. At 5:00 AM on the 3rd, they went to a courtyard of Xuzhou Middle School outside Beiguan and surrounded the inside and outside for security. Yi ordered the police to summon the five students Li, Li, Ma, Yao, and Liu, and immediately sent them to the county government for custody. The students rioted, so Yi summoned the students to the auditorium to read out the Department order. The students continued to clamor and shout, refusing to accept the Department order. Fearing that accidents might occur, Yi ordered the military police to withdraw and returned to the county government at 9:00 AM and telegraphed the province for instructions. The students in the second courtyard in the city did not participate. The students in custody were treated favorably in the Protection Committee. When the reporter interviewed Yi, Yi stated that the Department of Education had to take strict measures in order to maintain its authority and rectify the academic atmosphere. If the students obeyed the order and realized their mistakes, he would not want to sacrifice the youth's studies. He expressed his regret for the students' refusal to comply with the order and their arbitrary actions. Subsequent measures will be handled after receiving a telegram from the Department. The Department order is recorded as follows: "Case investigation of the Provincial Middle School senior high school normal department students, approaching the graduation period, there is a precedent for going out for visits. This year, during the national crisis, schools in the Beijing-Shanghai area have been affected by the war and cannot proceed as usual, and transportation in various places is mostly blocked. The order has been issued to various schools to stop all out-of-town visits. However, the Xuzhou Middle School senior high school normal department third-year students demanded to change their destination to Shandong and Beiping, threatening with a suspension of all classes and arbitrarily striking. After repeated persuasion by Principal Xue Zhongtai, the Department determined that the students' actions were out of line and ordered Principal Xue to investigate the instigators and submit them for punishment. Unexpectedly, the students of the grade not only did not repent but dared to expand the unrest, mobilizing the senior high school grades, occupying the two courtyards, expelling the principal and faculty from the school, and even threatening the entire junior high school to strike, cutting off transportation, and disrupting order. According to Principal Xue's personal report, it has been impossible to maintain the school. The senior high school students of the school have no regard for the law and insult their teachers. The circumstances are serious and should be severely punished in order to maintain discipline. The normal department third-year students Li Gaosong, Li Ruizhu, Ma Guangjun, Yao Hezhang, and Liu Haixi are identified by Principal Xue as the main instigators of the incident and should be taken into custody first pending investigation. All other third-year students in the department, except for those who requested leave for personal reasons, participated in the unrest after repeated persuasion. They are beyond redemption and should be expelled, and their deposits should be confiscated and their tuition and board fees recovered. The other senior high school grades that participated in the unrest and expanded the unrest should be temporarily disbanded for thorough rectification. The junior high school grades should immediately resume classes to emphasize their studies. For this reason, this supervisor is hereby ordered to go to the school to work with the principal to comply with this order and report for inspection. This order."

15th Anniversary of the Vocational Education Society

The 6th of this month is the 15th anniversary of the founding of the China Vocational Education Society. During the national crisis, there was no extravagant celebration. In addition to publishing the book "Theory and Practice of Vocational Education" on this day as a commemoration, only staff members of various departments and Shanghai members were gathered at the Workers' Education Center of the China Vocational School to hold a memorial ceremony. Members Zheng Tonghe, He Yushu, Hu Shuhua, Huang Fu, Shen Yi, Liu Zhanen, and others, as well as staff and students from affiliated organizations, nearly 2,000 people, attended. The meeting began at 9:00 AM with a flag-raising ceremony, followed by the whole assembly singing. Then, the groundbreaking ceremony for the addition of school buildings to the Vocational School was held, led by Mr. Zhu Ziqiao. After the ceremony, the meeting began. Cai Yuanpei and Jiang Wenyu gave opening speeches. Huang Renzhi and Yang Weiyu reported on the founding process of the Society, detailing the hardships of the Society's creation and the purpose of its establishment. Jia Foru, the current principal of the Vocational School, reported on the school's recent situation and the actual amount of donations for school buildings. Next, Shi Liangcai and Shen Xinqing, who have been directors for 15 consecutive years, as well as members Huang Yingbai and Huang Boqiao, gave speeches, describing the relationship between the Society's past work and the country and society, and the goals of future efforts. Mu Ouchu reported on the Society's recent work to save the country and presented souvenirs to Yao Huiquan and Zhu Weiyi for their efforts. Pan Xulun proposed the establishment of a large-scale vocational tutoring school as a 15th anniversary project, and Zhang Yunbo proposed launching a frugal national salvation movement. Both proposals were unanimously approved, and a committee was appointed to prepare for their implementation. Finally, Qian Xinzhi, chairman of the Society's board of directors, gave a reply, and the meeting was adjourned after a group photo was taken.

Shanghai University High School Holds Filial Piety Day

Since the opening of Shanghai Hujiang University in the city center, it has intensified its curriculum and focused on moral education. All school affairs are progressing as usual. It is reported that the school recently designated May 7 as Filial Piety Day to encourage students to respect their parents and follow their parents' guidance. At 11:50 AM yesterday, faculty, staff, and students gathered in the auditorium on Sichuan Road and invited the principal's wife, Mrs. Liu, to give a speech. She said that filial piety is an inherent Chinese virtue. She hoped that students would always consider how their parents love, care for, and educate their children, and not forget to be filial. They should also strive in their studies to live up to their family's expectations and extend their filial piety to love their country and nation. In this time of national crisis, we should be more determined to endure hardship and have a deep understanding. The meaning of the speech was profound and the words were very touching. After the speech, each person in attendance was presented with a flower to express the hope that parents would live long and symbolize remembrance.

Zhejiang Stadium Basketball Championship

Flying Horse Wins the Championship in the People's Group

(Hangzhou Express News) The Zhejiang Provincial Stadium launched the Hangzhou City Basketball Championship. Thirty-six teams from secondary and higher schools and people's organizations participated. Since it began on April 16, it has been held every Saturday and Sunday. The preliminary and semi-final rounds of the school group have not yet concluded, but the people's group concluded yesterday.

The Important Commemoration of Mother's Day

— Bi Yi

The Chinese Women's Temperance Association, with Mother's Day, commemorated by various countries on May 8th, approaching, has sent letters to its branches, requesting that mother-child gatherings be held on this day to promote the filial piety that the association has always advocated. It also prescribed various methods to express the affection of the younger generation towards their mothers. The intention is excellent. Some may say that the Book of Odes says, "Pitiful, pitiful are our parents, who bore me with such toil." It is the parents who should be commemorated. Since the toil is the same, it is appropriate to consider them equally and not to place undue emphasis on the mother. However, if one examines the reality, the mother's suffering in childbirth and raising children is even greater. A folk song from farming families says, "Ten months of pregnancy, the mother suffers; three years of breastfeeding, the mother toils." It is a true depiction. The saying, "A fake tune cannot compare to a real folk song," is indeed true. From these two phrases, one knows that the mother bears a greater responsibility than the father, so her kindness in toiling is even greater than the father's. Although the hardship of breastfeeding is often delegated to others by those who are able to hire a wet nurse, it is better for a child to be fed with its own mother's milk, as physiologists have explained in detail. Moreover, how can ordinary people without the means shirk this heavy responsibility? Mr. Gui Zhenchuan's "Biography of My Late Mother" is a piece that everyone reads and wants to weep. It says, "The older ones tug at her clothes, the younger ones are breastfed; the needlework in her hands never stops." The toil of poor mothers is vividly depicted. Furthermore, the hardship of pregnancy and the difficulty of childbirth cannot be avoided by anyone, whether noble or rich, who cannot shirk the responsibility of toiling and hire someone to replace them. Therefore, the commemoration of Mother's Day should be regarded as especially important. This is not just from the perspective of the Women's Association itself, but simply knowing that there is a mother. When it says that the association has always advocated filial piety, it means that the kindness of both parents is remembered.

On Danzig

— Kai Xu

Recently, according to European newspapers, Poland had an attempt to annex the Free City of Danzig, but it ultimately did not become a reality due to the intervention of neighboring countries. Afterwards, the Polish authorities and various related parties issued statements of clarification, stating that the rumors were groundless. The actions of fierce warlords in various countries around the world are all the same, invading people's lands and occupying them as their own. If the rumors were not without basis, the clarification would also be meddlesome. The Free City of Danzig is located on the southern coast of the Baltic Sea, with the Vistula River running through it, making it a central hub for European commerce and a strategically important place for land and naval military affairs. Surrounding powers, such as Germany, Russia, Poland, Prussia, Sweden, and Denmark, are all watching with covetous eyes, each wanting to fulfill their ambition to swallow it. However, Danzig, with its small area and 400,000 people, has been able to resist strong neighbors from outside its borders and maintain the dignity of an independent country. Alas, how does it compare to the demise of our three northeastern provinces in an instant? Danzig establishes a country with a single city, while our country has ten thousand times its area and cannot establish a country. In the Middle Ages, Danzig once fought England with thousands of undisciplined troops, defeated them, and captured the mayor of London, causing England not to dare to despise it for its small size for hundreds of years. Later, it was defeated once by Poland. Poland, with the prestige of victory, could have fulfilled its ambition to swallow it, but ultimately feared its people's spirit and allowed its independence. Between Poland and Danzig, they regarded each other as enemies. All documents between the Polish king and Danzig were mainly in Latin or German, and they never dared to use Polish. This is due to the unyielding spirit of the Teutonic people. Later, Poland was divided and perished by neighboring countries, but Danzig alone was able to maintain its autonomy. The people of Danzig are Germans, but the Germans also had no intention of annexing it. Later, based on the desire for national self-determination, it became attached to Germany. After World War I, Poland was restored, and Danzig was a port connecting Poland to the sea, but it was ultimately not given to Poland. It was only opened up as a belt area for Poland to access the sea and named the Polish Corridor. However, Poland found the corridor circuitous and inconvenient, so its ambition to annex Danzig never waned. But how could it achieve its wish? Alas, when I think of this, I cannot help but sigh deeply. I would rather be a free citizen of a small country than a slave of a large country.

Records of Polishing the Sword

Mr. Liang

— Gu Mingdao

Mr. Liang, I forget his name, was a neighbor's son in the past. He was physically strong and liked sports. At that time, the school had sports meets, and many people came to watch. Liang ran and jumped in the sports meet, repeatedly winning championships, showing off his manly skills. He was young and handsome, truly a lovable child. When the Xinhai Revolution army revolted in Wuchang, Liang rolled up his sleeves and said, "In the past, the young boy Wang Qi of Lu could take up arms to defend his country. Although I am young, I am older than Wang Qi. How can I not fulfill my duty as a citizen?" So he went to join the army secretly behind his family's back. He was in

Wuhan for several months, was wounded and returned. He regretted not being able to die on the battlefield. His family was surprised by this. From then on, Liang no longer sought education. When Mr. Niu Yongjian organized a student army in Songjiang during the Second Revolution, Liang again secretly went to join it. His family could not stop him. When the revolutionary army attacked the Shanghai Arsenal, the student army especially bravely charged forward, most of them sacrificing their lives under a hail of bullets. Liang was also among them. Unfortunately, the effort failed, and the student army disbanded invisibly. Liang's news disappeared without a trace. His family waited for his return, but he was not seen for a long time. They inquired everywhere but could not find out whether he was alive or dead. They thought that Liang had already sacrificed himself on the battlefield. Now, when the Shanghai War started, there were student armies participating, killing the enemy effectively and sacrificing themselves for the country. If Mr. Liang were still alive, he would surely roll up his sleeves and rise up again. How pitiful is this child!

Record of the Double Towers in Military Affairs (45)

— Master of the Seeking Happiness Studio

Chapter Six: Pitifully Forced into an Alliance Under the Bed in the Night of Shared Dreams; Still Remembering the Promise Neglected by the Window During First Love

Now, let's not rush into those things first. After you agree to my proposal, please first choose a date to announce our engagement and hold our wedding. Although you are currently in mourning, a large-scale event is a bit inconvenient, but inviting a few

close friends as witnesses and announcing it in the newspaper is essential to complete all the procedures, so that outsiders understand that this is a formal and legal marriage. Please give me a decision tonight so that it can be implemented as soon as possible. You shouldn't have any more excuses, right? As he spoke, he was composed and elegant, and lit another cigarette, waiting for An Yutian's answer. At this time, An Yutian had already been forced to surrender to the alliance under the bed and was preparing to submit a letter of surrender as soon as possible. However, upon hearing about the engagement and wedding, two pressing matters, he suddenly remembered Li Wenxia, who had made the same proposal the previous night. He couldn't help but secretly cry out in distress. This marriage is not a trivial matter. Once a promise has been made to one person, it cannot be lightly promised to a second person. It just so happened that the situation in these two days had become so strange, with one wave not yet settled and another rising. The first person was fiercely demanding the fulfillment of the old agreement and had not yet been properly dealt with, while the second person took the opportunity to propose a new alliance and was eager for a quick solution. Now he was in a dilemma and unable to take care of both. Surrendering to the second person in front of him would be like liking the new and forgetting the old. How would he deal with the first person in the future? If he insisted on prioritizing the old relationship and rejected the second person, he would regret his recklessness and falling into this dense spider web. In the end, there was no way to explain this rash act of defiling her purity for no reason. Moreover, he even thought of the serious time tonight, which was also the most important time he had agreed with Li Wenxia to wait for her at the apartment last night to discuss important matters together. How could the same kind of major event have replaced an opponent and a place for no reason, moving here to create new complications and joking with Liang Xiaoyun? And how could he have been so confused and forgotten his appointment with Li Wenxia last night in the past few hours, and relied on himself here to find even greater trouble? He truly couldn't forgive himself. He felt extremely sorry for both Li Wenxia and Liang Xiaoyun. For a moment, he was full of panic and drenched in sweat. He blurted out his heart's disease, saying, "This...this is fine, but I...I have done a terrible thing before. I had a promise of marriage with another woman. Now, it doesn't matter what formal actions you and I take. But that woman is not guaranteed not to have... objections."

Local Supplement (1) Shanghai Shen Bao Local Supplement

Introduction

Assassination Incidents

— Jin

Assassination is originally the most cruel and brutal thing, but in the aspect of using this means, people naturally think that there is "no way to go" and have no choice but to take this last resort. Unexpectedly, such cruel and brutal incidents would occur in three countries at the same time within two days, which is very unfortunate.

One, Paris, 6th dispatch: French President Doumer was attacked by a rioter today and shot five times in a row. Doumer was shot three times and has tragically died.

One, Madrid, 5th dispatch: The Spanish capital recently discovered a conspiracy to assassinate Prime Minister Aznar and an attempt to assassinate President Zamora.

One, Cairo, 6th dispatch: Egyptian Prime Minister Sidky and other famous politicians were traveling to Ghamra Station when a bomb exploded moments before, fortunately escaping unscathed.

Although the above three assassination cases have no connection, or belong to foreign countries, or belong to domestic countries, there is no need to discuss the causes and inside stories before clarifying the truth. But to put it in one sentence, it must contain political colors, it can be asserted.

According to today's newspaper, the murderer Go Guoloff who assassinated the French president confessed that during the European War, the White Russians participated in the war, which helped France a lot. Now that the White Russians have failed to this point, and France is standing by, not lending a hand, so he took this action. Whether this confession is reliable is unknown, but the White Russians have been miserably defeated, and the Red Russians have been in power for many years. Why only think of revenge today? It is very doubtful. The details of the other two cases are even more unknown.

However, the creation of an assassination case must have two objects. Party A wants to implement its own claims and refuses to accommodate Party B's claims, and Party B's claims have nowhere to be implemented, so they resort to this cruel and brutal means. This reason is very clear, so when an assassination case occurs, the politics of the country, whether foreign or domestic, must be in a state of precariousness. This is a clear and common rule.

The public has its own reasons, and the mother-in-law has her own reasons. Both sides and each has a reason. Is it the public's reason? Or is it the mother-in-law's reason? The right and wrong of both sides can be ignored. The public will definitely not accommodate the mother-in-law's claims, and the mother-in-law will definitely not accommodate the public's claims. Both sides cannot be open and honest, and work together in harmony, so the extremists have no other choice but to resort to this cruel means. This is also a definite and common rule.

I sincerely mourn the misfortune of the French president and am deeply worried about the general politicians.

Literature and Art

Two Poems Expressing Feelings

— Ge Chuan Kui

For five years, I have served in the English Department of the Commercial Press Translation Institute, associating with English classics every day, purchasing dozens of Western books, and writing several volumes of annotations on famous works. After the Shanghai Incident, everything was reduced to ashes. I was inspired to write this.

For years, I have been immersed in crab-like writing, loving to read Western books as if they were classics and tombs. How could I have known that Heaven would still be stingy with me, turning everything into ashes? What else is there to say?

Commenting on poems and essays takes a long time, carefully choosing words and phrases and spending time on thinking. If I had known that everything would become ashes today, I would laugh at myself for being too foolish in the beginning.

Science

Ink Manufacturing Method

By Nai Zheng

Ink is widely used. Whether it is teachers and students in schools or in business offices and writing rooms, they all need it. In the past, the ink on the market was all imported. In recent years, there has also been domestic ink production. Speaking of manufacturing ink, it is not a very difficult thing, but to make it very good, you must have a large capital to purchase machinery to manufacture it.

To make ink, you only need to slightly prepare glass utensils and other things as follows:

A soy sauce bottle, the finished ink can be stored inside. An old ink bottle, the ink is stored inside for writing. A funnel, a piece of summer cloth, a small enamel pot or basin, one or two small bamboo or wooden sticks. These tools are generally sufficient for making various inks.

Black Ink (Black Ink) Gallic Powder (Pulo Gallic) Four ounces (4oz) Boiling Water Two pounds (Q pint)

Iron Sulphate Solution (Solution) One and a half ounces (1 1/2 oz) Gum Arabic Three quarters of an ounce (3/4 oz) Creosote Two or three drops.

The above medicines can be bought in Western pharmacies or instrument stores. Together, their price is less than five dimes. But if you make it, it can turn into a soy sauce bottle.

The manufacturing is very convenient. We first soak the gallic powder in boiling water for one day and night. (If the water is cold, there is no need to add heat) Then take the summer cloth and filter it, put it in a small basin, and then take the ferrous sulfate, dissolve it in water, and after it is completely dissolved, you can put it in the small basin together, then add the gum arabic, and then stir it with a small stick to make it even, and at the same time add two or three drops of creosote. At this time, the ink is successful, and you can use a funnel to pour it into the soy sauce bottle for storage. When you use it, just pour some into the old ink, and when it's used up, pour some more. It's very convenient, but the old ink bottle must be thoroughly cleaned the first time. I will now introduce a blue ink as follows:

Gallic Powder, three and a half ounces, Indigo Sulfate, two and a half ounces, Iron Sulphate Solution, two and a half ounces, Cloves, a little, Gum Arabic, one and a half ounces, Clean water, two pounds (pints)

The method is exactly the same as above. Its color is a very beautiful blue and is very durable when written on paper.

Finally, I must explain clearly that these two formulas are probably from a book (Ink Manufacture), but it may not be this book. Recently, I happily went to a Western pharmacy to buy some medicines and went home to make them, but I was too impatient. The gallic was soaked in water, and I soaked it for the time I ate dinner, and then I added the other medicines. As a result, it was a great failure, the color was very light. Later, after studying it, I realized that the problem was that the gallic was not soaked thoroughly. The second time I did it was not bad, and the third and fourth times, I improved even more. As for the ingredients in the above formula, I have already slightly changed them, they are the ingredients of the best result. It is not very good to make them according to the ingredients in the English book. I think they will definitely not tell us the good ingredients. This point depends on one's own flexibility, research, experimentation, and improvement.

End of the Street

After the War

— Yu Xian

I happened to be strolling on Nanjing Road.

Nanjing Road is still Nanjing Road before the war. The stylish cars seem to be running like a busy street. The Indian Sikh is still brandishing his stick and hitting the backs of rickshaw pullers. In the huge glass windows, eye-catching advertisements are decorated. Of course, the electric lights are lit very beautifully day and night, and our young masters and misses are also wearing novel clothes, adding a lot of color to the spring in Shanghai.

There are no traces of war here.

I happened to be strolling on Minguo Road.

Minguo Road will restore Minguo Road before the war. The iron sheds are opening one after another. The Chinese who took refuge in the concession during the war have moved back. The stores have opened. (Never mind their long-term resistance and painful opening) The most notable thing is that the barbed wire and sandbags have disappeared unconsciously.

There will be no traces of war here.

I dare not go to Wusong to take a walk.

I am afraid that the painful traces will always remain, causing me a bad feeling.

Birth

What I Saw at the Bund Park

— Ying Dai

Although you can't see a trace of national disaster on the faces of lovers, men and women, and the soldiers of country X, from the pedestrians on the road and the audience in the movie theaters, the spring travelers by the West Lake and on Longhua Road this year are still colder than in previous years, right? In the past three months, even I, who have nothing to do with family or country, have felt no desire to go for a spring outing and no desire to see a movie. It was not until the afternoon of the day before yesterday that I happened to pass through the Bund and took the opportunity to spend two dimes to take a walk in the Bund Park and breathe some relatively fresh air.

However, it would have been better not to go in. After walking in, I got quite a few sad impressions. Everything in the Bund Park still remains unchanged from the past. The red flowers and green trees clearly tell me that the god of spring has descended for a long time. Blue-eyed, high-nosed Western men, holding slender-waisted, full-breasted Western women, walk straight in the park. Of course, the majority of the tourists in the park are our Chinese, men, women, old and young. Their faces are filled with smiles and are whispering sweet nothings.

Among these tourists, the most noticeable are of course those Westernized modern men and women. Pairs of them, hand in hand, shoulder to shoulder, sit on iron-framed chairs, either making eye contact or looking at the scenery across the river. During this period of late spring and early summer, it is naturally an unparalleled pleasure in life to tour the red peach blossoms and green willows with a lover, and to exchange endless sweet nothings. Where do they still think of Zhabei being invaded and Wusong being forcibly seized?

Leaning on the iron railing, looking across the river, our line of sight, as long as it shoots to the center of the river, will see several ships of country X moored in the gray and yellow waves. The flag of country X is fluttering in the wind. The ships are full of joyful air. Some are singing victorious military songs loudly. Inconsistent songs are faintly sent into my eardrums from afar. Some are looking at everything on the riverside on the deck. Their line of sight may sometimes come into contact with the people in the park, revealing an arrogant attitude, mocking us Chinese who have nothing.

How embarrassing, how sad, my tears couldn't help but flow down. Let's go, I really don't want to see this kind of scene anymore.

There Are

True or False?

— Wu Wei

The day before yesterday, I went to the theater to have tea. Three tea drinkers came to the table next to me. I heard some wonderful theories, no, maybe it was nonsense.

A: When China and Japan were at war, the City God, Lord Guan, and Lord Yue were all helping in the sky.

B: Oh, no wonder the enemy kept suffering defeats... But, how do you know?

A: The Pure Yang Patriarch said it when he descended on the altar in our neighbor's spirit medium temple...

C: Yes, when the fighting was tight, I went to the City God Temple to ask for a divination stick. For more than five minutes, the stick wouldn't fall out!...

B: What happened then?

C: Later, the incense keeper told me to wait a moment. He told me that the City God was very busy recently and often went out...

A: How long did you wait then?

C: Later, I waited for a full twenty minutes. The incense keeper said he was here, and told me to look at the City God's forehead, which had a lot of sweat on it?...

A: Really?

C: Of course, I saw it with my own eyes.

B: Oh, no wonder my wife bought a piece of tin foil and a few pairs of straw sandals once and said she would take them to the City God Temple to burn. She also said that the neighbor told her that the City God had entrusted a dream to the incense keeper saying that he wanted silver and straw sandals. I didn't believe it at first...

"..................." I heard this and saw that the sky seemed to be about to rain, so I got up and left.

Inconceivable

A Few Words

— Xin Xiu

Last Saturday night, I visited a friend. Several friends were gathered at his house, talking about the status of their respective industries after the Songhu War. I sat down and listened quietly.

The manager of a domestic goods cloth wholesale store shook his head and frowned, saying, "It's terrible. Those of us who rely on selling cloth from this factory are really going to starve to death. Usually, the sales of factory cloth, except in those places where the customs are not very open, and the generally unadorned people who value simplicity still welcome it, the more so-called civilized ports, the less people ask about domestic goods cloth. But I thought that after this painful Shanghai Incident, the general public would be stimulated like this, and the sales of our factory cloth might have a turning point. Who knew that the business of Wang Laohe was still thriving!"

Wang Laohe replied with a smile, "Not necessarily. However, the newly arrived batches of patterned cloths have very good colors and patterns, so sales may be better. I most envy Mr. Zhang, whose business is the best. As long as you get a light-on license, regardless of whether the market is good or bad, the general old guns always patronize every day, rain or shine. This is simply better than opening a rice shop. Those unemployed poor people who have no money to buy rice and cook can also muddle through a meal with a few coppers. However, this problem of 'eating black rice' is much more difficult than 'eating white rice.' When the addiction comes, it's truly like 'mourning one's parents,' with tears and snot, very sad. Therefore, Mr. Zhang's store is always full of guests every day, and profits triple!"

Mr. Zhang smiled and said to a young man in a suit, "The most developed business is your industry! Look, among the 400 million people in the country now, let alone a few, there are 200 million people who smoke cigarettes. It's truly become so widespread, regardless of the rich or poor, men or women, old or young! If we make a statistic of the money we spend on cigarettes throughout the year, the total amount must be surprisingly large! Compared with our industry, it's simply incomparable."

Mr. Li, the bookstore manager, sighed, "Everyone's business is good, but my book business is truly a bitter meal. Usually, except for a portion of romance, love, and sex books that still have some sales, the rest of the textbooks and literary books are simply unattended all day long. We sit in the store, watching the generally student-like young men in suits and modern ladies go to dance halls and movie theaters, all passing us by without entering - now we don't even have enough for daily expenses. What should we do?"

When everyone heard this, they were all listless and went back separately.

Bamboo Root

Drifting

— Zhu Lai

Due to the war, the word "drifting" has unfortunately been added to our lives.

Originally, living a drifting life is a great misfortune in life. Usually, when I see groups of drifters on the street, I hate that social undertakings are declining and cannot accommodate those young and useful people. On the one hand, I think they are self-indulgent, so they are ostracized by society, but at the same time, I deeply feel the pain of unemployment. Because they are unfortunate and unemployed, they turn into drifters. If our rice bowl is broken, aren't we the same as them? Therefore, those who wander on the thorny road of society are all filled with the terror of drifting.

The day before the flames of war engulfed Zhabei, I was originally preparing to go to school to attend class, but upon hearing the unfortunate news, I returned home dejectedly. From then on, I drifted all day long in villages with rows of green willows, drifted in fields of yellow flowers and green wheat, drifted on avenues with fragrant grass. However, such drifting also allowed me to appreciate a flavor, enough to wash away all the miscellaneous thoughts in my heart. It can truly be said to be joy in suffering.

The wind is getting tighter. I boarded a small boat and went to Chongming, drifting for twenty days. I ate the exotic dishes there, saw the famous scenic spots there, and the schools and customs of Chongming were all deeply imprinted in my ears and eyes. Such drifting made me almost think I was in a foreign country, not knowing that the west of the Huangpu River was already under the iron hooves of the Japanese.

Movies

Unprecedented Color Spectacle to Premiere in Nanjing: The grand movie "The Art of Love," depicting a gold-digging woman on Broadway in New York, is scheduled to premiere today at the Nanjing Grand Theater. The entire film is rendered in the latest scientific and beautiful colors, vibrant and bright, setting a new record for color films. The film tells the romantic story of a Broadway showgirl, full of extreme joy and sorrow, interspersed with Broadway's glamorous dances and famous songs, exposing New York's nightlife vividly and luxuriously, stirring the heart. The leading actors are Mary Brian and Marian Nixon. Mary is known as Hollywood's charming and innocent actress, with excellent expressions and a great reputation. Marian Nixon is the leading actress in the popular film "Reckless," known for her flirtatious performances. Now, she meets the Shanghai public again in this film, and it is hoped that she will receive an enthusiastic welcome.

"Parisian Rendezvous" to Be Released: Nicknamed "Throaty Jenny" Jeanette MacDonald has gained great fame since "The Love Parade." She has produced many works since then, but most recently, "Parisian Rendezvous" is considered her most successful. The play will be released today at the Paris Grand Theater. The plot is sad and poignant, the performance is delicate and unparalleled, and the clear song is like an oriole leaving the valley, captivating the audience. In addition, the famous star Joe E. Brown co-stars, adding to the beauty. In addition, there are spectacular scenes such as snowy landscapes and plane crashes, which add a lot to the drama.

"Zhengqi Bao" Expands Coverage: "Zhengqi Bao," organized by Meihuaguan Master, was previously published as a temporary special edition due to the impact of the war. Now that peace has been achieved and the market is gradually recovering, the original coverage will be restored from today, and the content will be greatly refreshed. Out-of-town subscribers can subscribe to the newspaper at its office in Yuren Lane, Yunnan Road, this city.

Corrections

In the May 1st issue, there was a sentence saying "Xu Xilin's rule." According to Xu, he was the superintendent of the Higher Police School. This is incorrect. Also, in the May 4th issue, there was a sentence saying "also advocated sexology." The word "xue" (學, study) was a typo for "ting" (霆). Also, in the May 6th issue, there was a sentence saying "life has increased very much." The word "ji" (即, immediately) was a typo for "yu" (慾, desire). We hereby make these corrections. Also, in the four words "die xiong dang fu" (疊胸蕩服), the "die" (疊, piled) was a typo for "tu" (突, protruding), and "fu" (服, clothes) was a typo for "gu" (股, thighs).

Jiangsu High Court Second Branch

Civil Judgments: ▲ A case of Sheng Zhongtian vs. Dacheng Silk Store Guo Junshan in a lawsuit over repayment of goods. (Main text) The appeal is rejected, and the appellant bears the second-instance litigation costs. ▲ A case of Yang Shen Yanzhang vs. Yang Houquan in a lawsuit over debt. (Main text) The appeal is rejected, and the appellant bears the second-instance litigation costs. ▲ A case of Xu Shuibao's younger brother vs. Xu Lianqing in a lawsuit over cohabitation and divorce. (Main text) The appeal is rejected, and the appellant bears the second-instance litigation costs. ▲ Criminal Judgments: ▲ A case of Zhang Shiming et al. for kidnapping for ransom and robbery. (Main text) The original judgment regarding Zhang Shiming's robbery conviction and sentence is reversed. Zhang Shiming is sentenced to twelve years for robbery. Combined with the original sentence for kidnapping for ransom, the death penalty shall be executed. The remaining appeals are rejected. ▲ A case of Zhang Yunshan for breach of trust. (Main text) The appeal is rejected. ▲ A case of Zhou Qiqian et al. for robbery. (Main text) The original judgment regarding Zhou Qiqian and Wang Er is reversed. Zhou Qiqian is sentenced to seven years and six months for each of the two robbery charges, with a combined sentence of eight years. Wang Er is sentenced to ten years and six months for each of the four robbery charges, with a combined sentence of twelve years. The number of days of detention before the judgment is confirmed shall be deducted from the prison sentence at a rate of two days per day. ▲ A case of Sha Guifu for attempted premeditated murder. (Main text) The appeal is rejected.

Civil Ruling: ▲ A case of Lin Zhongqin vs. Wang Jiansheng in a lawsuit over the settlement of mortgage funds. Because Lin Zhongqin's whereabouts are unknown and documents cannot be served, the appellee Wang Jiansheng has requested public service.

Civil Judgment: ▲ A case of the Eastern Provincial Railway Business Office et al. vs. Zhenxiang Firm Yang Tongzeng in a lawsuit over compensation. (Main text) The original judgment regarding the amount of compensation is changed. The Eastern Provincial Railway Business Office shall compensate the appellee with silver totaling 22,002 taels, 2 mace, and 4 fen. The remaining appeals are rejected. The appellants bear 9/10 of the second-instance litigation costs, and the appellee bears 1/10.

Public Service: ▲ A case of Chen Yikang vs. Hefeng Bank in a lawsuit over debt. (Main text) The appeal is rejected, and the appellant bears the second-instance litigation costs. (May 7th)

Shanghai First Special District Local Court Announcement

Regarding the announcement of the auction, this court is enforcing a case of Yuan Chengzhuang, the creditor, versus Jie Meisheng, the debtor, in a lawsuit over a mortgage. The debtor's property listed below has been sealed and appraised. The auction date is set for May 16th. The court will dispatch a clerk to direct the bailiff to conduct the auction. Residents who wish to purchase the property should report to the bailiff's office of this court to inspect the property at its location and then bid on time. If there are two or more bidders, the person with the highest bid will be the buyer. The full price must be paid on the spot, and the auctioned property will be given to the buyer for receipt. Residents are hereby informed. The details are as follows: (1) Object of the auction: Two pieces of jewelry. (2) Location of the object: This court. (3) Minimum price: 1,800 yuan. (4) Place to view the record: This court's bailiff office. (5) Enforcement Clerk Zhu Guangzhao, Bailiff Liu Yulin.

Regarding the announcement of the auction, this court is enforcing a case of Jigui Firm et al., the creditors, versus Wu Zhongtang, the debtor, in a lawsuit over the price of goods. The debtor's property listed below has been sealed and appraised. The auction date is set for May 14th. The court will dispatch a clerk to direct the bailiff to implement the auction together with the bailiffs. Residents who wish to purchase the property should immediately report to the bailiff's office of this court to inspect the property at its location and then bid on time. If there are two or more bidders, the person with the highest bid will be the buyer. The full price must be paid on the spot, and the auctioned property will be given to the buyer for receipt. Residents are hereby informed. The details are as follows: (1) Object of the auction: Movable property (a separate list is available). (2) Location of the object: Xinwanxiang Tea and Wheat Shop on Xiaoshadu Road, Laowanxiang Southern Goods Shop, and Xinwanxiang Snacks Workshop. (3) Minimum price: 126 yuan and 1 jiao. (4) Place to view the record: This court's bailiff office. (5) Enforcement Clerk Wang Zhen, Bailiff Wang Ai Xuan.

Shanghai First Special District Local Court

Civil First Instance Judgments:

Li Kuanji vs. Feng Fang, Manager of Qichang, Monetary Case (Main Text):

The defendant shall repay the plaintiff 1,149 taels and 5 mace. The litigation fee shall be borne by the defendant.

Zhou Xuehai vs. Yuan Moqin, Divorce Case (Main Text):

The plaintiff's claim is rejected. The litigation fee shall be borne by the plaintiff.

Zhang Miaoji vs. Wang Zhiqing, Debt Case (Main Text):

The petition is rejected. The petition fee shall be borne by the petitioner.

Dickson vs. Ren Bangyan, Repayment Case (Main Text):

The defendant shall return to the plaintiff 1,299 taels and 5 mace of silver, and 1,051 yuan and 05 cents in silver dollars. The remainder of the plaintiff's claim is rejected. The litigation fee shall be borne by the defendant for two-thirds and by the plaintiff for one-third.

Peng Sheng vs. Zhou Asong et al., Debt Case (Main Text):

The defendant Zhou Asong shall repay the plaintiff 200 yuan. If he cannot repay, the defendant Shen Abao shall repay on his behalf. The litigation fee shall be borne by the defendant Zhou Asong.

Yifeng Foreign Firm (Abraham) vs. Ma Dehong et al., Rent Case (Main Text):

The defendant Ma Dehong shall repay the plaintiff's rent of 101 taels. The defendant Zhang Dezhong is responsible for clearing and repaying this rent. If he cannot repay, the principal of the defendant Anyu Firm shall repay on his behalf. The plaintiff's claim against the defendant Xie Kechang is rejected. The litigation fee shall be borne by the defendants Ma Dehong and Zhang Dezhong.

Qi Beisheng vs. Yang Chunji, Debt Case (Main Text):

The defendant Yang Chunji shall repay the plaintiff 80 yuan. If he cannot repay, the defendant Chen Jinsi shall repay on his behalf. The litigation fee shall be borne by the defendant Yang Chunji.

Sun Dasheng vs. Zhu Wenguang, Loan Case (Main Text):

The defendant Zhu Wenguang shall repay the plaintiff 60 yuan. If he does not comply, the defendant Li Jincai shall be responsible for repaying on his behalf. The litigation fee shall be borne by the defendant Zhu Wenguang.

Lun Sheng vs. Wang Buchan et al., Debt Case (Main Text):

The defendants shall jointly repay the plaintiff 280 yuan. This amount shall be repaid at 40 yuan per month until fully repaid. The litigation fee shall be borne jointly by the defendants.

Bai Dingsheng vs. Zheng Abao et al., Loan Case (Main Text):

The defendant Zheng Abao shall repay the plaintiff 122 yuan. If he does not comply, the defendant Yao Zhiming shall be responsible for repaying on his behalf. The litigation fee shall be borne by the defendant Zheng Abao.

Bai Jinsheng vs. Shi Mingji et al., Loan Case (Main Text):

Shi Mingji shall repay the plaintiff 150 yuan. If he does not comply, the defendant Yao Dade shall be responsible for repaying on his behalf. The litigation fee shall be borne by the defendant Shi Mingji.

Mao Tianshui vs. Yagoloff et al., Debt Case (Main Text):

The defendant Yagoloff shall repay the plaintiff 85 yuan. If he does not comply, the defendant Fan Siliayev shall be responsible for repaying on his behalf. The litigation fee shall be borne by the defendant Yagoloff.

Xu Zhibei vs. Yongjiang Restaurant, Debt Case (Main Text):

The defendant shall repay the plaintiff 71 yuan and 6 jiao for goods. The litigation fee related to the defendant's part of the lawsuit shall be borne by the defendant.

Song Rongchuan vs. Sun Liechang, Claim for Deposit Case (Main Text):

The defendant shall pay the plaintiff 2,300 taels of silver, plus interest calculated monthly at 1% from February 1, 1932, until the date of payment. The litigation fee shall be borne by the defendant.

Tonghe Company vs. Ma Yuxing Firm (Ma Zhigang), Rent Case:

The defendant shall repay the plaintiff's rent arrears of 1,900 yuan and vacate the premises. The litigation fee shall be borne by the defendant.

Shanghai Second Special District Local Court

Civil Judgement: Wei Wenzeng v. Meikelie Candy Store for Debt Repayment Case (Main Text): The defendant shall repay the plaintiff the amount of $499 in silver dollars. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant. ▲ Yang Yan v. Xu Rongsheng for Damages and Incidental Civil Suit (Main Text): The defendant shall compensate the plaintiff for damages amounting to $452 in silver dollars. The remaining claims of the plaintiff are rejected. The litigation costs shall be borne equally by both parties.

Civil Instructions: One case: Qin Binggen et al. petition for a temporary suspension of the public auction of Huang Chu Jiu Hospital. Upon reviewing the petition, it is noted that this court, due to a petition from the Shanghai New Medicine Trade Association to purchase Huang Chu Jiu Hospital, held a hearing on April 29th of this year. After the agents of both parties agreed to first announce a public auction of the real estate, it was decided that if no higher bid was received, the association would be allowed to purchase it. As this method does not harm the interests of creditors, it is not appropriate to change it again. The petitioner's request for a temporary suspension of the public auction and a copy of the Shanghai New Medicine Trade Association's petition for investigation shall not be considered. This instruction. ▲ One case: Kingsbury et al. request registration for adopting a young girl. Upon reviewing the petition, this instruction. ▲ One case: Chen Fengbao petitions to withdraw the judgment of exclusion. Upon reviewing the petition, permission is granted to withdraw the petition. Let the defendant Wei Maogou be informed. ▲ Regarding public notice of service, in the case of Yang Tingzhang v. Shanghai Local Court

Criminal Judgement: Zhang Mingchu et al. v. Yang Jiangshi et al. for Theft and Stolen Goods Case (Main Text): Xu Jingou and Cai Shigui are both innocent. The self-prosecution of Xu Danshi is not accepted. Yang Jiangshi is sentenced to two months of imprisonment for assisting in the purchase of stolen goods. The number of days of detention shall be offset against the imprisonment at a rate of two days per day. ▲ Guan Yuanming is sentenced to five months of imprisonment for knowingly purchasing stolen goods. The number of days of detention shall be offset against the imprisonment at a rate of two days per day. The four boxes of pork are confiscated. ▲ Yao Peijun Opium Appeal Case (Main Text): The original judgment regarding the crime and sentence is revoked. Yao Peijun is sentenced to one month of imprisonment for smoking opium and is fined 100 yuan. If the fine is not fully paid after compulsory execution, one day of imprisonment shall be substituted for every three yuan. The number of days of detention shall be offset against the imprisonment at a rate of two days per day. ▲ Ruling on Guan Yuanming's request to suspend detention (Main Text): This request is rejected.

Civil Instructions: Zhu Songquan et al. petition for the execution of Gu Wenqing. Upon reviewing the petition, it is noted that the conciliation record states that if Gu Wenqing fails to repay the debt by the due date, the petitioners shall be liable for the repayment. Since the debt is due and Gu Wenqing has not repaid it, execution should be carried out against the petitioners. The request to continue executing against Gu Wenqing shall not be considered. This instruction. ▲ Ding Jiaqiu et al. petition for combined execution. Upon reviewing the petition, it is noted that the parties in Case No. 26 of the Land Division in the 20th year and Case No. 1051 of the Land Division in the 19th year are different. Execution should be carried out separately. The request for combined execution is not approved. This instruction. ▲ The agent of Chen Shundetang petitions for the sealing of all real estate. Upon reviewing the petition, it is noted that the compulsory execution in this case is under the name of Wang Huating's debt. The shared property outside the name of the debtor cannot be sealed together. The request shall not be considered. This instruction.

Criminal Judgement: Kang Xinming v. Embezzlement and Public Danger Case (Main Text): Kang Xinming is sentenced to six months of imprisonment for the crime of embezzling other people's property in his possession with the intention of illegal possession for himself. The number of days of detention shall be offset against the imprisonment at a rate of two days per day. ▲ Chen Fengshan is sentenced to four months of imprisonment for the crime of jointly selling military rifle stocks and bullets without permission. The number of days of detention shall be offset against the imprisonment at a rate of two days per day. ▲ Zhu Zhaolong Opium Case (Main Text): Zhu Zhaolong is fined ninety yuan for possessing opium with the intention of using it for criminal purposes. If the fine is not fully paid after compulsory execution, one day of imprisonment shall be substituted for every one yuan. The number of days of detention shall be offset against the imprisonment at a rate of two days per day. 17 taels of opium are confiscated and burned. ▲ Yin Alin et al. Assault Case (Main Text): Yin Alin, Bian Keming, and Lu Maosheng are each fined forty yuan for jointly causing bodily harm. If the fine is not fully paid after compulsory execution, one day of detention shall be substituted for every one yuan. The number of days of detention shall be offset against the fine at a rate of one day per yuan. ▲ Cheng Yanan et al. Opium and Forgery Appeal Case (Main Text): The original judgment is revoked. Cheng Yanan and Zhang Zhongji are innocent.

The number of days of detention shall be offset against the imprisonment at a rate of two days per day. ▲ You Asi Opium Case (Main Text): You Asi is sentenced to six months of imprisonment and fined 180 yuan for assisting in the possession of opium with the intention to sell. If the fine is not fully paid after compulsory execution, one day of imprisonment shall be substituted for every one yuan. The number of days of detention shall be offset against the imprisonment at a rate of two days per day. 230 taels of opium are confiscated and burned. ▲ Chen Xigui Opium Case (Main Text): Chen Xigui is sentenced to six months of imprisonment and fined 30 yuan for selling opium substitutes. If the fine is not fully paid after compulsory execution, one day of imprisonment shall be substituted for every two yuan. The number of days of detention shall be offset against the imprisonment at a rate of two days per day. ▲ Li Hanqing Theft Case (Main Text): Li Hanqing is sentenced to six months of imprisonment for stealing during a disaster. The number of days of detention shall be offset against the imprisonment at a rate of two days per day. ▲ Feng Langqiu Embezzlement Case (Main Text): Feng Langqiu is sentenced to six months of imprisonment for embezzling other people's property in his possession with the intention of illegal possession for himself. The number of days of detention shall be offset against the imprisonment at a rate of two days per day. ▲ Zhu Jiquan Theft Case (Main Text): Zhu Jiquan is sentenced to four months of imprisonment for theft. The number of days of detention shall be offset against the imprisonment at a rate of two days per day.
